  write_cframe (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.include.node_modules.@rbxts.dl-modfile-packager.out.serialize.property.util.write_cframe

    local t = {

    	[1] = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0),

    	[5] = Vector3.new(0, 0, -1)
    }
    return {
    	write_cframe = {
    		write = function(p1, p2) --[[ writeCFrame | Line: 10 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]
    			local UpVector = p2.UpVector
    			local RightVector = p2.RightVector
    				local v3 = t[i]
    				if 1 - v3:Dot(RightVector) < 0.0001 then
    					v1 = i
    				if 1 - v3:Dot(UpVector) < 0.0001 then
    					v2 = i
    				local Position = p2.Position
    				p1.writeByte(v1 * 6 + v2)
    				p1.writeFloat32(Position.X)
    				p1.writeFloat32(Position.Y)
    				p1.writeFloat32(Position.Z)

    				local v4, v5, v6, v7, v8, v9, v10, v11, v12, v13, v14, v15 = p2:GetComponents()

    				p1.writeFloat32(v14)
    				p1.writeFloat32(v15)
    		read = function(p1) --[[ readCFrame | Line: 61 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]
    			local v1 = p1.readByte()
    				return CFrame.new(p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32(), p1.readFloat32())

    				local v3 = t[v1 % 6]
    				local v4 = v2:Cross(v3)

    }
